4/9/24, 3:42â€¯PM - +91 98281 97248: UiPath Apps Academic Challenge 2024
*About the Project*
The UiPath Apps Academic Challenge 2024 is an exciting opportunity for university students to showcase their innovation and problem-solving skills using UiPath Apps, a low-code application development platform. This challenge invites students from diverse academic backgrounds to create impactful applications that address real-world problems, automate processes, and drive digital transformation.

Participants will have the chance to explore the capabilities of UiPath Apps and unleash their creativity to develop practical solutions in various domains such as education, healthcare, finance, sustainability, and more. Whether it's streamlining administrative tasks, enhancing communication channels, or improving data analysis, students are encouraged to leverage the power of automation to make a positive impact.

Throughout the challenge, participants will receive guidance, resources, and support to help them develop their projects effectively. They will have the opportunity to collaborate with peers, learn from industry experts, and gain valuable hands-on experience in application development and automation.

The UiPath Apps Academic Challenge 2024 aims to inspire and empower the next generation of innovators, equipping them with the skills and knowledge to thrive in a rapidly evolving digital landscape.

Join us on this exciting journey to revolutionize the way we work, learn, and live through the power of UiPath Apps.
4/9/24, 3:42â€¯PM - +91 98281 97248: Rules and Guidelines
*Participation Rules and Guidelines*
 
Eligibility: Participants must be currently enrolled as full-time university students. Teams can comprise individuals or groups, but each member must meet the eligibility criteria.

Registration: All participants must register through the official website before the registration deadline. Late entries will not be accepted.

Original Work: Submissions must be the original work of the participants. Plagiarism or unauthorized use of others' work will result in disqualification.

Code of Conduct: Participants must adhere to a code of conduct, promoting respectful and ethical behavior throughout the challenge.

Language: All submissions and communications must be in English.
4/9/24, 3:42â€¯PM - +91 98281 97248: *Project Requirements, Submission Format, and Judging Criteria:*
 
Project Requirements: Projects must be developed using UiPath Apps and aligned with the theme of "Empowering Change through Automation." They should address a real-world problem and demonstrate innovative use of automation.

Submission Format: Submissions must include a project description, screenshots, a demonstration video, and any necessary documentation. Detailed submission guidelines will be provided closer to the submission deadline.

Judging Criteria: Projects will be evaluated based on creativity, technical proficiency, innovation, impact, and alignment with the theme. Judges will also consider the clarity of presentation and documentation.

Scoring: Each project will be scored based on predefined criteria, and the highest-scoring projects will advance to the final round.
4/9/24, 3:42â€¯PM - +91 98281 97248: *Restrictions and Limitations:*
 
Team Size: Teams can consist of a maximum of 4 members with 1 faculty as mentor

Multiple Entries: Participants or teams may submit only one project for consideration.

Use of UiPath Apps: Projects must be developed using UiPath Apps. Integrations with other platforms or tools are allowed but must be clearly documented.

Legal Compliance: Submissions must comply with all applicable laws and regulations, including copyright and intellectual property rights.

10/15/24, 10:39â€¯AM - +91 98878 52862: *Sample Question*

A solid cube of 10 cm x 10cm x 10 cm rests on the ground.  It has a beetle on it, and some sweet honey spots at various locations on the surface of the cube.  The beetle starts at a point on the surface of the cube, and goes to the honey spots in order along the surface of the cube.

Problem Description
A solid cube of 10 cm x 10cm x 10 cm rests on the ground.  It has a beetle on it, and some sweet honey spots at various locations on the surface of the cube.  The beetle starts at a point on the surface of the cube, and goes to the honey spots in order along the surface of the cube.

1.      If it goes from a point to another point on the same face (say X to Y), it goes in an arc of a circle that subtends an angle of 60 degrees at the centre of the circle

2.      If it goes from one point to another on a different face, it goes by the shortest path on the surface of the cube, except that it never travels along the bottom of the cube

The beetle is a student of Cartesian geometry, and knows the coordinates (x, y, z) of all the points it needs to go to.  The origin of coordinates it uses is one corner of the cube on the ground, and the z axis points up.  Hence, the bottom surface (on which it does not crawl) is z=0, and the top surface is z=10.  The beetle keeps track of all the distances travelled, and rounds the distance travelled to two decimal places once it reaches the next spot, so that the final distance is a sum of the rounded distances from spot to spot.


Input
The first line gives an integer N, the total number of points (including the starting point) the beetle visits

The second line is a set of 3N comma separated non-negative numbers, with up to two decimal places each.  These are to be interpreted in groups of three as the x, y, z coordinates of the points the beetle needs to visit in the given order.

Output
One line with a number giving the total distance travelled by the beetle accurate to two decimal places.  Even if the distance travelled is an integer, the output should have two decimal places.

Constraints
None of the points the beetle visits is on the bottom face (z=0) or on any of the edges of the cube (the lines where two faces meet)

2<=N<=10

Difficulty Level
Complex

Time Limit (secs)
1

Examples
Example 1

Input

3

1,1,10,2,1,10,0,1,9

Output

4.05

Explanation

There are three points visited by the beetle (N=3). The beetle starts on the top face of the cube (z=10) at point (1,1,10) and goes to another point on the same face (2,1,10).  Though the straight line distance is 1, it travels on the arc of a circle subtending an angle of 60 degrees at the centre of the circle, and hence travels (2*pi)/6 or 1.05 (note that it rounds the distance at each leg of the journey).  It then travels from (2,1,10) on the face z=10 to (0,1,9) on the face x=0 along the surface of the cube. This is a distance of 3.  The total distance travelled is 1.05+3=4.05.  The output is 4.05

Example 2

Input

3

1,1,10,2,1,10,0,5,9

Output

6.05

Explanation

There are three points visited by the beetle (N=3). The beetle starts on the top face of the cube (z=10) at point (1,1,10) and goes to another point on the same face (2,1,10).  As before. This distance is 1.05.   It then travels from (2,1,10) on the face z=10 to (0,5,9) on the face x=0 along the surface of the cube. The shortest distance on the surface of the cube between these points is 5.  The total distance travelled is 1.05+5=6.05.  The output is 6.05.

2/5/25, 2:08â€¯PM - +91 93140 99002: Dear Students,
Soft skills or behavioural skills are not learnt through books or Google or OTT series. 
They are habits that need to be inculcated and developed through experiential learning . 
Each interaction leads to knowing yourself better. 
Each experience leads to your self development. 

You must now be more focused on your behaviour improvement. 

*Behavioural improvement*
1)doesn't  mean you have a bad behaviour. 
It means you need to work on developing your behaviour while working in an organisation. 
2) Discipline 
3).Self awareness 
4) Ownership and responsibility 
5)presentation skills 
6) Interaction and confidence 
7) Spoken and written communication 
8) body language 
9) people dealing skills 

These are the crust of soft skills that had over 300 sub topics. 
These skills are learnt through training and practicing practical. 
Like you going to gym to improve your physical  appearance and strength 

Soft skills refine's  your mental, emotional and physical appearance . Making you a better version of yourself. 
Give yourself the opportunity to be better. 
You are responsible for your career,your tomorrow and your family's happiness 
Make your parents proud by reaching the highest possibilities in your career. 

If you understand this you will never miss any opportunity to learn.

Thanks 
Winfred Crawford

ğŸ”¹ Stage 1 (Online Qualification Round): A jeopardy-style Capture The Flag (CTF) challenge covering Web Attacks, Network Exploitation, API Vulnerabilities, OT SCADA, and more.
